@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("Leave blank to skip a provider.")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        prompt_text = f"{info['description']} [{env_var}]"

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"[{provider}] Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(prompt_text, default="", show_default=False)
        if new_key:
            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    click.secho("Setup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', required=True, help="Model name (e.g., gpt-4o, claude-3-5-sonnet, zenmux/glm-4)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)
                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
        reply = response.choices[0].message.content

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        usage_data = {}
        if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
            if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
            elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                usage_data = response.usage.dict()
            else:
                try:
                    usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                except Exception:
                    usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            click.echo("-" * 40)
            click.echo(reply)
            click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("Leave blank to skip a provider.")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        prompt_text = f"{info['description']} [{env_var}]"

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"[{provider}] Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(prompt_text, default="", show_default=False)
        if new_key:
            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    click.secho("Setup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', required=True, help="Model name (e.g., gpt-4o, claude-3-5-sonnet, zenmux/glm-4)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)
                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
        reply = response.choices[0].message.content

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        usage_data = {}
        if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
            if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
            elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                usage_data = response.usage.dict()
            else:
                try:
                    usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                except Exception:
                    usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            click.echo("-" * 40)
            click.echo(reply)
            click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

import sys
import json
import datetime
import re
from pathlib import Path

import click
from dotenv import load_dotenv, set_key

env_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / '.env'
if env_path.exists():
    load_dotenv(dotenv_path=env_path)

PROVIDERS = {
    "ZENMUX": {
        "env_var": "ZENMUX_API_KEY",
        "description": "ZenMux API Key (provides free GLM 5.2 and others)",

@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("Leave blank to skip a provider.")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        prompt_text = f"{info['description']} [{env_var}]"

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"[{provider}] Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(prompt_text, default="", show_default=False)
        if new_key:
            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    click.secho("Setup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', required=True, help="Model name (e.g., gpt-4o, claude-3-5-sonnet, zenmux/glm-4)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)
                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
        reply = response.choices[0].message.content

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        usage_data = {}
        if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
            if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
            elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                usage_data = response.usage.dict()
            else:
                try:
                    usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                except Exception:
                    usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            click.echo("-" * 40)
            click.echo(reply)
            click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## Response
Looking at `walkie.py`, I'll suggest 3 high-impact improvements to make it more robust and Antigravity IDE agent-friendly:

## 1. **Automatic .env Bootstrapping with Security**
The current setup requires manual intervention. Add auto-bootstrapping that creates `.env` from `.env.example` if it exists, with proper permissions.

## 2. **Stream Output Option**
Add streaming support for real-time token delivery, which is crucial for IDE agents to show progressive results and handle long responses efficiently.

## 3. **Provider Verification & Fallback Chain**
Add pre-flight verification and a fallback mechanism to try alternative providers when the primary one fails, making the tool more resilient.

Here are the concrete diffs:

### Improvement 3: Provider Verification & Fallback Chain
```diff

+def verify_provider(provider_name):
+    """Pre-flight check to verify provider connectivity."""
+    info = PROVIDERS.get(provider_name.upper())
+    if not info:
+        return False, "Unknown provider"
+    
+    api_key = os.getenv(info["env_var"])
+    if not api_key:
+        return False, "API key not configured"
+    
+    import litellm
+    try:
+        kwargs = {
+            "model": info["test_model"],
+            "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "ping"}],
+            "max_tokens": 2,
+            "api_key": api_key
+        }
+        if info.get("api_base"):
+            kwargs["api_base"] = info["api_base"]
+        
+        litellm.completion(**kwargs)
+        return True, "OK"
+    except Exception as e:
+        return False, str(e)
+
+FALLBACK_CHAINS = {
+    "zenmux/": ["ZENMUX", "OPENROUTER", "OPENAI"],
+    "nvidia/": ["NVIDIA", "OPENROUTER", "OPENAI"],
+    "openai/": ["OPENAI", "OPENROUTER", "ZENMUX"],
+    "anthropic/": ["ANTHROPIC", "OPENROUTER"],
+}
+
+def determine_fallback_model(model, original_api_base):
+    """If primary provider fails, determine a fallback model."""
+    for prefix, chain in FALLBACK_CHAINS.items():
+        if model.startswith(prefix):
+            for provider in chain[1:]:  # Skip the first (already failed)
+                info = PROVIDERS.get(provider)
+                if info and os.getenv(info["env_var"]):
+                    if provider == "OPENROUTER":
+                        return f"openrouter/{model.split('/')[-1]}", None, os.getenv(info["env_var"])
+                    else:
+                        return info["test_model"], info.get("api_base"), os.getenv(info["env_var"])
+            break
+    return None, None, None

# Walkie-Talkie Log

**Date:** 2026-07-08_09-57-56
**Model:** nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2

## User Prompt
We want to optimize walkie.py. Specifically, please provide code improvements for:
1. Better Attachment Chunking/Truncation: Instead of cutting characters directly in the middle of lines (e.g. file_content[:max_chars]), slice it strictly at a newline boundary. Ensure the truncated block includes an explicit message stating the number of lines/characters truncated and that no lines were cut mid-line.
2. Friendly and Secure Setup: Guide users interactively on where and how to obtain API keys (e.g., ZenMux, NVIDIA NIM, Groq, Gemini) during 'walkie setup', validate that the entered keys are not empty or malformed (e.g., matching common key patterns), and enforce high safety (secure .env permissions chmod 0600 on Unix, and masking inputs during key entry). if env_path.exists():
    load_dotenv(dotenv_path=env_path)
else:

    example_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / '.env.example'
    if example_path.exists():
        import shutil
        try:
            shutil.copy(example_path, env_path)

        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Warning: Failed to bootstrap .env: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)

PROVIDERS = {

@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("Leave blank to skip a provider.")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        prompt_text = f"{info['description']} [{env_var}]"

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"[{provider}] Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(prompt_text, default="", show_default=False)
        if new_key:
            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    click.secho("Setup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', required=True, help="Model name (e.g., gpt-4o, claude-3-5-sonnet, zenmux/glm-4)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Determine max characters allowed for attachments based on model context limit
    # 1 token ≈ 4 characters in English text / code
    max_chars = 300000  # Default: ~100k tokens (120k tokens context window)
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000  # 1M+ context
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000  # 200k context
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000   # 8k context (safety limit)
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000   # 16k context

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                # Context-aware chunking/truncating specifically to different models
                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    file_content = file_content[:max_chars]
                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated from {original_len} to {max_chars} characters.",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )
                    file_content += "\n\n... [TRUNCATED DUE TO MODEL CONTEXT WINDOW LIMIT] ..."

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n### Attached Files Context:\n" + "\n".join(attachment_blocks)

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            # Extract usage safely
            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                    delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                    if hasattr(delta, 'content') and delta.content:
                        content_chunk = delta.content
                        chunks.append(content_chunk)
                        if not json_output:
                            click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        # Logging
        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        # Save MD
        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        # Output result
        if not json_output:
            if not stream:  # Avoid printing delimiters/content twice if already streamed
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## Response
Here are the code improvements addressing both of your requests.

### 1. Better Attachment Chunking/Truncation
We replace the naive character slicing (`file_content[:max_chars]`) with a safe boundary-based slicing. It will search for the next newline character after the threshold limit to ensure no lines are chopped mid-line, and append a precise truncation notice.

### 2. Friendly and Secure Setup
We introduce `getpass` for secure masked key entry, regex-based validation for common provider key patterns (e.g., `sk-` for OpenAI, `grod_` style prefixes, length checks), and explicit guidance on where to fetch keys. We also strictly enforce high file safety with `chmod 0600`.

Antigravity IDE agents will parse this as part of the response or fail to extract clean code.\n- The logging logic (`click.secho(\"Logged to...\")`) writes to `stderr`, which is good, but the file paths and markdown logs clutter the workspace unnecessarily for an agent.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Add a `--quiet` or `--raw` flag that disables all `click.secho` and visual separators, printing *only* the LLM response to `stdout`.\n- Conditionally save logs to a temp directory (e.g., `tempfile.gettempdir()`) instead of a local `./logs` folder if `--raw` is passed, preventing workspace pollution.\n\n### 3. Security & API safety\n**Weaknesses:**\n- **Regex Key Validation Fails:** The script bundles strict regex patterns for keys. If a provider changes their key format (e.g., OpenAI recently changed their key format), the script will prevent the user from saving a valid key.\n- **Secrets Leakage in Logs:** The `./logs` directory saves the exact system prompt and user prompt in JSON and Markdown formats. If a user pipes environment variables or secrets into the prompt, they are written to disk in plaintext.\n- **`.env` permissions:** The script enforces `0o600` on Linux but ignores Windows ACLs.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Remove the strict regex block during setup, or make it a soft warning that doesn't block saving.\n- Add a `--no-log` flag to prevent writing prompts to disk entirely.\n- Redact or hash sensitive information in logs, or add a warning in `setup`.\n\n### 4. Token & context window efficiency\n**Weaknesses:**\n- Hardcoded `max_chars` mapping (`300000`, `2000000`, `20000`) is brittle. Groq's context windows have expanded beyond 8k, and Gemini 1.5 Pro actually supports 2M+ tokens (approx 8M chars).\n- The comment stripping regex (`_strip_comments`) is risky. It can easily break Python code if a `#` appears inside a string, or remove TypeScript compiler directives (`/// <reference path=\"... />`).\n- Attachments are concatenated via simple string interpolation (`full_prompt += \"\\n\\n...`), which doesn't optimize for the model's specific vision/code parsing capabilities.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Use `litellm.token_counter(model=...)` instead of calculating via hardcoded characters.\n- Remove the custom `_strip_comments` function or replace it with a proper AST-based parser for Python and a dedicated lexer for JS/TS, rather than regex.\n\n### 5. Streaming reliability\n**Weaknesses:**\n- The streaming loop expects `chunk.choices[0].delta.content`. Some providers (like Anthropic via LiteLLM) might send empty choice deltas or use different attributes, leading to `IndexError` or `AttributeError`.\n- If the stream drops mid-way, the script catches the exception, but anything printed to `stdout` is already out there. It might confuse the IDE agent.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Use `litellm.utils.get_streaming_response` or wrap the chunk parsing in safer `getattr` and boundary checks.\n\n### 6. Robust error handling\n**Weaknesses:**\n- `sys.exit(1)` on API error kills the process, which is bad for Antigravity if it's running the script in a persistent shell.\n- The `route_model` function references `NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY` but it's not defined anywhere in the `PROVIDERS` dictionary or setup script.\n- Exception catches are too broad (`except Exception`). Network timeouts vs. Authentication failures vs. Context Window overflows should be handled distinctively.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Catch `litellm.APIError`, `litellm.AuthenticationError`, and `litellm.Timeout` explicitly.\n- Fix the missing DeepSeek env var reference.\n\n### 7. Piping & automation integration\n**Weaknesses:**\n- Parsing of `--extra-body` uses `json.loads`, which is fine, but if a user pipes a JSON string via stdin alongside a prompt, it fails.\n- `sys.stdin.isatty()` logic is synchronous and can block if no input is provided in some weird shell environments.\n- The CLI prints `------` separators in non-JSON modes. If an IDE pipes the output, it gets `--------\\nCode\\n--------` which it then has to regex out.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Ensure that if `--json-output` is passed, *no* other text goes to `stdout`.\n- Drop the `---` separators entirely in non-streaming mode, or make them opt-in.\n\n### 8. Logging & diagnostics\n**Weaknesses:**\n- Writing logs to `./logs` folder relative to the current working directory is dangerous. If run from `/`, it tries to write to `/logs`.\n- The generated Markdown log doesn't format the response as a code block, making it hard to read in Markdown viewers.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Use `Path.home() / \".walkie\" / \"logs\"` to centralize logs.\n- Wrap the response in ` ``` ` in the markdown log.\n\n### 9. Provider extensibility\n**Weaknesses:**\n- `route_model` hardcodes `if model.startswith(\"zenmux/\"):` etc. If you add a new provider, you have to edit the routing logic manually.\n- `PROVIDERS` and `PROVIDER_CONFIG` are separated. They should be merged into a single dictionary to avoid desync.\n\n**Suggestions:**\n- Unify the provider dictionaries.\n- Rely on LiteLLM's native prefixing (`provider/model`) and simply pass `api_base` via the `PROVIDERS` dict dynamically without hardcoded `if/else` blocks.\n\n### 10. @click.group()

    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', required=True, help="Model name (e.g., gpt-4o, claude-3-5-sonnet, zenmux/glm-4)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Determine max characters allowed for attachments based on model context limit
    # 1 token ≈ 4 characters in English text / code
    max_chars = 300000  # Default: ~100k tokens (120k tokens context window)
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000  # 1M+ context
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000  # 200k context
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000   # 8k context (safety limit)
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000   # 16k context

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                # Context-aware chunking/truncating specifically to different models
                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    # Find the first newline boundary after max_chars to keep lines complete
                    trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = len(file_content)

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                    delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                    if hasattr(delta, 'content') and delta.content:
                        content_chunk = delta.content
                        chunks.append(content_chunk)
                        if not json_output:
                            click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            if not stream:
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## Response
Here is a comprehensive audit of `walkie.py` across the 10 requested perspectives, identifying weaknesses and providing concrete suggestions and code diffs.

### 1. Non-tech user friendliness
**Weaknesses:**
- Users have to remember exact provider prefixes (e.g., `zenmux/`, `nvidia/`) to route models correctly. 
- The `setup` command requires a terminal. GUI users might struggle with hidden password prompts.
- Default models are not provided for the `ask` command, requiring users to know exact model slugs.

**Suggestions:**
- Implement a fallback model in `ask` (e.g., default to `gpt-3.5-turbo` or `openrouter/auto`).
- Add a `walkie models` command that prints out available providers and their `test_model` slugs so users know what to type.

### 2. Antigravity IDE agent compatibility
**Weaknesses:**
- The CLI inserts a lot of human-readable noise into `stderr` and `stdout` (e.g., `Calling {model}...`, `Streaming...`, `----` separators). Antigravity IDE agents will parse this as part of the response or fail to extract clean code.
- The logging logic (`click.secho("Logged to...")`) writes to `stderr`, which is good, but the file paths and markdown logs clutter the workspace unnecessarily for an agent.

**Suggestions:**
- Add a `--quiet` or `--raw` flag that disables all `click.secho` and visual separators, printing *only* the LLM response to `stdout`.
- Conditionally save logs to a temp directory (e.g., `tempfile.gettempdir()`) instead of a local `./logs` folder if `--raw` is passed, preventing workspace pollution.

### 3. Security & API safety
**Weaknesses:**
- **Regex Key Validation Fails:** The script bundles strict regex patterns for keys. If a provider changes their key format (e.g., OpenAI recently changed their key format), the script will prevent the user from saving a valid key.
- **Secrets Leakage in Logs:** The `./logs` directory saves the exact system prompt and user prompt in JSON and Markdown formats. If a user pipes environment variables or secrets into the prompt, they are written to disk in plaintext.
- **`.env` permissions:** The script enforces `0o600` on Linux but ignores Windows ACLs.

**Suggestions:**
- Remove the strict regex block during setup, or make it a soft warning that doesn't block saving.
- Add a `--no-log` flag to prevent writing prompts to disk entirely.
- Redact or hash sensitive information in logs, or add a warning in `setup`.

### 4. Token & context window efficiency
**Weaknesses:**
- Hardcoded `max_chars` mapping (`300000`, `2000000`, `20000`) is brittle. Groq's context windows have expanded beyond 8k, and Gemini 1.5 Pro actually supports 2M+ tokens (approx 8M chars).
- The comment stripping regex (`_strip_comments`) is risky. It can easily break Python code if a `#` appears inside a string, or remove TypeScript compiler directives (`/// <reference path="... />`).
- Attachments are concatenated via simple string interpolation (`full_prompt += "\n\n...`), which doesn't optimize for the model's specific vision/code parsing capabilities.

**Suggestions:**
- Use `litellm.token_counter(model=...)` instead of calculating via hardcoded characters.
- Remove the custom `_strip_comments` function or replace it with a proper AST-based parser for Python and a dedicated lexer for JS/TS, rather than regex.

### 5. Streaming reliability
**Weaknesses:**
- The streaming loop expects `chunk.choices[0].delta.content`. Some providers (like Anthropic via LiteLLM) might send empty choice deltas or use different attributes, leading to `IndexError` or `AttributeError`.
- If the stream drops mid-way, the script catches the exception, but anything printed to `stdout` is already out there. It might confuse the IDE agent.

**Suggestions:**
- Use `litellm.utils.get_streaming_response` or wrap the chunk parsing in safer `getattr` and boundary checks.

### 6. Robust error handling
**Weaknesses:**
- `sys.exit(1)` on API error kills the process, which is bad for Antigravity if it's running the script in a persistent shell.
- The `route_model` function references `NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY` but it's not defined anywhere in the `PROVIDERS` dictionary or setup script.
- Exception catches are too broad (`except Exception`). Network timeouts vs. Authentication failures vs. Context Window overflows should be handled distinctively.

**Suggestions:**
- Catch `litellm.APIError`, `litellm.AuthenticationError`, and `litellm.Timeout` explicitly.
- Fix the missing DeepSeek env var reference.

### 7. Piping & automation integration
**Weaknesses:**
- Parsing of `--extra-body` uses `json.loads`, which is fine, but if a user pipes a JSON string via stdin alongside a prompt, it fails.
- `sys.stdin.isatty()` logic is synchronous and can block if no input is provided in some weird shell environments.
- The CLI prints `------` separators in non-JSON modes. If an IDE pipes the output, it gets `--------\nCode\n--------` which it then has to regex out.

**Suggestions:**
- Ensure that if `--json-output` is passed, *no* other text goes to `stdout`.
- Drop the `---` separators entirely in non-streaming mode, or make them opt-in.

### 8. Logging & diagnostics
**Weaknesses:**
- Writing logs to `./logs` folder relative to the current working directory is dangerous. If run from `/`, it tries to write to `/logs`.
- The generated Markdown log doesn't format the response as a code block, making it hard to read in Markdown viewers.

**Suggestions:**
- Use `Path.home() / ".walkie" / "logs"` to centralize logs.
- Wrap the response in ` ``` ` in the markdown log.

### 9. Provider extensibility
**Weaknesses:**
- `route_model` hardcodes `if model.startswith("zenmux/"):` etc. If you add a new provider, you have to edit the routing logic manually.
- `PROVIDERS` and `PROVIDER_CONFIG` are separated. They should be merged into a single dictionary to avoid desync.

**Suggestions:**
- Unify the provider dictionaries.
- Rely on LiteLLM's native prefixing (`provider/model`) and simply pass `api_base` via the `PROVIDERS` dict dynamically without hardcoded `if/else` blocks.

### 10. Code quality & maintainability
**Weaknesses:**
- The script uses top-level `import litellm` inside command functions. This is slow if the user runs `walkie --help`.
- `os.chmod` and `shutil.copy` are logic that belong in a setup utility class.
- There's a missing newline string concatenation: `full_prompt += "\n\n` is followed immediately by `import litellm`.

**Suggestions:**
- Move `import litellm` to the top of the file or use a lazy-loading caching mechanism.
- Merge the configuration dictionaries.

---

### Suggested Code Diff / Refinements

Here is a patched version of critical sections addressing the above:

PROVIDERS = {
    "ZENMUX": {
        "env_var": "ZENMUX_API_KEY",

def route_model(model):
    """Dynamically route models based on provider prefix."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None
    routed_model = model

    if "/" in model:
        prefix = model.split("/")[0].upper()
        provider_info = PROVIDERS.get(prefix)
        if provider_info:
            api_base = provider_info.get("api_base")
            api_key = os.getenv(provider_info["env_var"])
            # If it's a custom base, LiteLLM usually expects just the model name 
            # or the openai/ prefix depending on the api. 
            if api_base and prefix != "OPENROUTER":
                routed_model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]

    return routed_model, api_base, api_key

            if system and not raw: # Avoid logging secrets
