    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', required=True, help="Model name (e.g., gpt-4o, claude-3-5-sonnet, zenmux/glm-4)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Determine max characters allowed for attachments based on model context limit
    # 1 token ≈ 4 characters in English text / code
    max_chars = 300000  # Default: ~100k tokens (120k tokens context window)
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000  # 1M+ context
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000  # 200k context
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000   # 8k context (safety limit)
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000   # 16k context

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                # Context-aware chunking/truncating specifically to different models
                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    # Find the first newline boundary after max_chars to keep lines complete
                    trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = len(file_content)

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                    delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                    if hasattr(delta, 'content') and delta.content:
                        content_chunk = delta.content
                        chunks.append(content_chunk)
                        if not json_output:
                            click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            if not stream:
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## Response
Here's a comprehensive audit of `walkie.py` across all 10 perspectives:

## 1. Non-tech User Friendliness

**Weaknesses:**
- Setup command requires understanding of API keys and providers
- Error messages use technical terms without plain-language explanations
- No progress indication during long operations
- Missing `--help` examples for common use cases
- No idle timeout indication for streaming

**Suggested Improvements:**
```python

    # ... rest of setup code
```

```python

## 2. Antigravity IDE Agent Compatibility

**Weaknesses:**
- Uses `click` which may conflict with IDE terminal integration
- No machine-readable output format for IDE parsing
- `sys.exit(1)` breaks IDE agent workflows
- No dry-run mode for IDE testing

**Suggested Improvements:**
```python
@cli.command()
@click.option('--output-format', type=click.Choice(['text', 'json', 'ide']), 
              default='text', help="Output format for IDE integration")
@click.option('--dry-run', is_flag=True, help="Preview without making API calls")
def ask(model, prompt, output_format='text', dry_run=False, **kwargs):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    if dry_run:
        click.echo(json.dumps({
            "status": "dry_run",
            "model": model,
            "prompt_length": len(prompt),
            "would_charge": True
        }))
        return  # Don't sys.exit, just return
    
    try:
        # ... main logic
        if output_format == 'ide':
            click.echo(json.dumps({
                "success": True,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "error": None
            }))
        # ... rest of output handling
    except Exception as e:
        if output_format == 'ide':
            click.echo(json.dumps({
                "success": False,
                "error": str(e),
                "error_type": type(e).__name__
            }))
        raise click.ClickException(str(e))  # Instead of sys.exit
```

## 3. Security & API Safety

**Weaknesses (Critical):**
- API keys passed directly in kwargs - no secure storage mechanism
- Logs contain full prompts and responses (potential secrets leak)
- No rate limiting or request validation
- `extra_body` parameter allows arbitrary JSON injection
- `os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)` has race condition

**Suggested Improvements:**
```python
# Secure key retrieval
def get_api_key(provider):
    """Retrieve API key with fallback to keyring."""
    import keyring
    env_key = os.getenv(PROVIDERS[provider]["env_var"])
    if env_key:
        return env_key
    try:
        return keyring.get_password("walkie-talkie", provider.lower())
    except:
        return None

# Sanitize logs to prevent secret leakage
def sanitize_log_data(log_data):
    """Remove potential secrets from log data."""
    sensitive_patterns = [
        r'(?i)(api[_-]?key|token|secret|password|auth)[\s:=]+[^\s\n]+',
        r'sk-[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{20,}',
        r'AIzaSy[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{33}'
    ]
    sanitized = json.dumps(log_data)
    for pattern in sensitive_patterns:
        sanitized = re.sub(pattern, '[REDACTED]', sanitized)
    return json.loads(sanitized)
```

```python
# Rate limiting
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class RateLimiter:
    def __init__(self, max_requests=60, window_seconds=60):
        self.requests = []
        self.max_requests = max_requests
        self.window = timedelta(seconds=window_seconds)
    
    def can_proceed(self):
        now = datetime.now()
        self.requests = [r for r in self.requests if now - r < self.window]
        if len(self.requests) >= self.max_requests:
            return False
        self.requests.append(now)
        return True

rate_limiter = RateLimiter()

# In ask() function:
if not rate_limiter.can_proceed():
    click.secho("Rate limit exceeded. Please wait before making another request.", 
                fg="red", err=True)
    sys.exit(1)
```

## 4. Token & Context Window Efficiency

**Weaknesses:**
- Character-based truncation is inaccurate (uses 4 chars = 1 token)
- No message pruning for long conversations
- Attachment handling doesn't consider total prompt length
- Missing model-specific system prompt length limits

**Suggested Improvements:**
```python
import tiktoken

def estimate_tokens(text, model="gpt-4"):
    """Accurate token estimation using model-specific encodings."""
    try:
        if model.startswith("claude"):
            # Claude uses ~5 chars per token for English
            return len(text) // 5
        encoding = tiktoken.encoding_for_model(model)
        return len(encoding.encode(text))
    except:
        return len(text) // 4  # Fallback

def fit_to_context_window(messages, model, max_output_tokens=None):
    """Ensure messages fit within model's context window."""
    MODEL_CONTEXT_LIMITS = {
        "gpt-3.5-turbo": 4096,
        "gpt-4": 8192,
        "claude-3-haiku": 200000,
        "gemini-1.5-flash": 1000000,
    }
    
    model_limit = MODEL_CONTEXT_LIMITS.get(model.split('/')[-1], 128000)
    if max_output_tokens:
        available = model_limit - max_output_tokens
    else:
        available = model_limit - 500  # Reserve for response
    
    total_tokens = sum(estimate_tokens(m["content"], model) for m in messages)
    
    while total_tokens > available and len(messages) > 1:
        removed = messages.pop(1)  # Keep system message
        total_tokens -= estimate_tokens(removed["content"], model)
    
    return messages
```

## 5. Streaming Reliability

**Weaknesses:**
- No reconnection logic for broken streams
- `nl=False` in click.echo may buffer incorrectly
- Missing signal handling (Ctrl+C during stream)
- No timeout for stalled streams

**Suggested Improvements:**
```python
import signal
import time

class StreamHandler:
    def __init__(self, timeout=30):
        self.timeout = timeout
        self.last_chunk_time = time.time()
        self.interrupted = False
        signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self.handle_interrupt)
    
    def handle_interrupt(self, signum, frame):
        self.interrupted = True
        click.echo("\nStream interrupted by user.", err=True)
    
    def process_chunk(self, chunk):
        self.last_chunk_time = time.time()
        if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
            delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
            if hasattr(delta, 'content') and delta.content:
                return delta.content
        return None
    
    def check_timeout(self):
        if time.time() - self.last_chunk_time > self.timeout:
            raise TimeoutError("Stream stalled - no chunks received")

# Usage in ask():
stream_handler = StreamHandler()
response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)

try:
    for chunk in response_stream:
        if stream_handler.interrupted:
            click.echo("\n[Stream interrupted - partial response saved]", err=True)
            break
        
        stream_handler.check_timeout()
        content = stream_handler.process_chunk(chunk)
        if content:
            chunks.append(content)
            click.echo(content, nl=False)
            sys.stdout.flush()  # Ensure immediate output
except TimeoutError as e:
    click.secho(f"\nStream error: {e}", fg="red", err=True)
```

## 6. Robust Error Handling

**Weaknesses:**
- Generic exception catching hides specific failure modes
- No retry logic for transient failures
- Missing file permission and encoding error handling
- `errors='ignore'` in file reading silently corrupts data

**Suggested Improvements:**
```python
from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_exponential

class APIError(Exception):
    pass

class ConfigurationError(Exception):
    pass

@retry(
    stop=stop_after_attempt(3),
    wait=wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10),
    retry=retry_if_exception_type((ConnectionError, TimeoutError))
)
def make_api_call(**kwargs):
    """Make API call with retry logic for transient errors."""
    try:
        response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
        return response
    except litellm.exceptions.AuthenticationError as e:
        raise ConfigurationError(f"API key invalid or expired: {e}")
    except litellm.exceptions.RateLimitError as e:
        raise APIError(f"Rate limit exceeded: {e}")
    except litellm.exceptions.ServiceUnavailableError as e:
        raise ConnectionError(f"Service unavailable: {e}")
    except Exception as e:
        raise APIError(f"Unexpected API error: {e}")

# File reading with explicit encoding detection
def read_file_safely(file_path, encodings=['utf-8', 'latin-1', 'cp1252']):
    """Attempt to read file with multiple encodings."""
    for encoding in encodings:
        try:
            with open(file_path, 'r', encoding=encoding) as f:
                return f.read()
        except UnicodeDecodeError:
            continue
        except PermissionError:
            raise click.BadParameter(f"No permission to read {file_path}")
    raise click.BadParameter(f"Could not decode {file_path} with any encoding")
```

**Weaknesses:**
- Exit codes don't differentiate error types
- JSON output mixes with status messages on stderr
- No structured error output for automation
- Missing batch processing capability

**Suggested Improvements:**
```python
# Structured exit codes for automation
class ExitCodes:
    SUCCESS



================================================================================
FILE: logs\2026-07-08_13-09-25_nvidia-z-ai-glm-5.2.json
================================================================================
{
  "timestamp": "2026-07-08_13-09-25",
  "model": "nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2",
  "routed_model": "openai/z-ai/glm-5.2",
  "system_prompt": "",
  "user_prompt": "Audit the attached walkie.py script in 10 perspectives:\n1. Non-tech user friendliness\n2. Antigravity IDE agent compatibility\n3. Security & API safety\n4. Token & context window efficiency\n5. Streaming reliability\n6. Robust error handling\n7. Piping & automation integration\n8. Logging & diagnostics\n9. Provider extensibility\n10.   "response": "Here is an audit of `walkie.py` across the 10 requested perspectives, along with concrete weaknesses, suggestions, and a unified code diff to address them.\n\n### 1. Non-tech user friendliness\n* **Weakness**: If a user double-clicks the script or runs it without arguments, it prints the generic Click help and exits. The `setup` command lacks a clear test-all or skip-all functionality.\n* **Suggestion**: Add a default fallback that launches `setup` if no arguments are provided. Add a visual progress indicator in `setup`.\n\n### 2. Antigravity IDE agent compatibility\n* **Weakness**: When `--json-output` is used, the script interleaves unstructured text and colored ANSI escape codes into `stderr` (`Calling {model}...`). IDEs and automated agents parsing `stdout` for JSON might accidentally capture this noise if they combine streams.\n* **Suggestion**: Ensure all human-readable progress updates are cleanly isolated to `stderr` and cleanly separated from the mathematical JSON payload on `stdout`.\n\n### 3. Security & API safety\n* **Weakness**: The `.env` file is created in the script directory (`Path(__file__).resolve().parent / '.env'`). When installed globally via `pip`, this writes `.env` to system `site-packages`. \n* **Suggestion**: Store `.env` in the current working directory (`Path.cwd() / '.env'`) or the user's home directory (`Path.home() / '.walkie.env'`).\n\n### 4. Token & context window efficiency\n* **Weakness**: The `_strip_comments` function is a naive regex-based comment remover. It will happily corrupt code by mistaking comment-like syntax inside strings for actual comments, or fail on nested multiline strings. \n* **Suggestion**: While naive stripping is light, it's safer to properly tokenize. However, for a lightweight CLI, use a safer regex or warn the user that aggressive stripping might modify string literals.\n\n### 5. Streaming reliability\n* **Weakness**: The script has `except Exception: pass` inside the streaming loop, silently eating network errors or malformed chunks. If the stream drops midway, the user gets a partial output with no warning.\n* **Suggestion**: Catch specific exceptions, append a system warning to the output, and optionally allow the script to finish with an error exit code instead of silently passing.\n\n### 6. Robust error handling\n* **Weakness**: The script writes logs to a hard-coded `logs/` directory relative to the current working directory. If the user runs the script from a read-only directory, it crashes. \n* **Suggestion**: Use a centralized logging path (e.g., `Path.home() / '.walkie' / 'logs'`) and handle directory creation safely.\n\n### 7. Piping & automation integration\n* **Weakness**: When streaming text (without `--json-output`), a hard-coded closure string (`\"-\" * 40`) is appended to the end of the stream. If a user pipes `walkie ask --stream` into another command, the hyphens corrupt the output. \n* **Suggestion**: Omit UI decorations completely when `sys.stdout.isatty()` is `False`. \n\n### 8. Logging & diagnostics\n* **Weakness**: Currently, full prompt contents and full responses are logged to JSON and markdown files. For long context windows (e.g., 1M tokens), a single query can generate hundreds of megabytes of logs, filling the disk. \n* **Suggestion**: Add a `--no-log` flag to disable logging for high-volume/automated queries, and an environment variable override for the log directory.\n\n### 9. Provider extensibility\n* **Weakness**: `route_model` has a hardcoded `if/elif` block for ZenMux, NVIDIA, and other custom prefixes. Adding a new provider requires modifying the core routing logic. \n* **Suggestion**: Tie routing to the `PROVIDERS` dictionary. If a model starts with a provider prefix, dynamically pick the `api_base` and `api_key` from the config rather than hardcoding it.\n\n### 10. Code quality & maintainability\n* **Weakness**: The `ask` command is a 150-line monolith handling stdin parsing, file reading, chunking, routing, API calls, and logging. \n* **Suggestion**: Break it down into helper functions (`build_prompt`, `handle_streaming`, `log_interaction`). \n\n---\n\n### Unified Code Diff / Refactoring\n\nBelow is the updated code applying these improvements:\n\n```py\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport json\nimport datetime\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nimport click\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv, set_key\n\n# 3.         import shutil

            shutil.copy(example_path, env_path)

@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', default="nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2", help="Model name (defaults to nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Determine max characters allowed for attachments based on model context limit
    # 1 token ≈ 4 characters in English text / code
    max_chars = 300000  # Default: ~100k tokens (120k tokens context window)
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000  # 1M+ context
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000  # 200k context
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000   # 8k context (safety limit)
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000   # 16k context

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                # Context-aware chunking/truncating specifically to different models
                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    # Find the nearest newline boundary strictly under max_chars to keep lines complete
                    trunc_idx = file_content.rfind('\n', 0, max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        # Fallback to finding the first newline after max_chars if none exists before it
                        trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = max_chars

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                try:
                    if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                        delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                        content_chunk = getattr(delta, 'content', None)
                        if content_chunk:
                            chunks.append(content_chunk)
                            if not json_output:
                                click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            if not stream:
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## Response
Here is an audit of `walkie.py` across the 10 requested perspectives, along with concrete weaknesses, suggestions, and a unified code diff to address them.

### 1. Non-tech user friendliness
* **Weakness**: If a user double-clicks the script or runs it without arguments, it prints the generic Click help and exits. The `setup` command lacks a clear test-all or skip-all functionality.
* **Suggestion**: Add a default fallback that launches `setup` if no arguments are provided. Add a visual progress indicator in `setup`.

### 2. Antigravity IDE agent compatibility
* **Weakness**: When `--json-output` is used, the script interleaves unstructured text and colored ANSI escape codes into `stderr` (`Calling {model}...`). IDEs and automated agents parsing `stdout` for JSON might accidentally capture this noise if they combine streams.
* **Suggestion**: Ensure all human-readable progress updates are cleanly isolated to `stderr` and cleanly separated from the mathematical JSON payload on `stdout`.

### 3. Security & API safety
* **Weakness**: The `.env` file is created in the script directory (`Path(__file__).resolve().parent / '.env'`). When installed globally via `pip`, this writes `.env` to system `site-packages`. 
* **Suggestion**: Store `.env` in the current working directory (`Path.cwd() / '.env'`) or the user's home directory (`Path.home() / '.walkie.env'`).

### 4. Token & context window efficiency
* **Weakness**: The `_strip_comments` function is a naive regex-based comment remover. It will happily corrupt code by mistaking comment-like syntax inside strings for actual comments, or fail on nested multiline strings. 
* **Suggestion**: While naive stripping is light, it's safer to properly tokenize. However, for a lightweight CLI, use a safer regex or warn the user that aggressive stripping might modify string literals.

### 5. Streaming reliability
* **Weakness**: The script has `except Exception: pass` inside the streaming loop, silently eating network errors or malformed chunks. If the stream drops midway, the user gets a partial output with no warning.
* **Suggestion**: Catch specific exceptions, append a system warning to the output, and optionally allow the script to finish with an error exit code instead of silently passing.

### 6. Robust error handling
* **Weakness**: The script writes logs to a hard-coded `logs/` directory relative to the current working directory. If the user runs the script from a read-only directory, it crashes. 
* **Suggestion**: Use a centralized logging path (e.g., `Path.home() / '.walkie' / 'logs'`) and handle directory creation safely.

### 7. Piping & automation integration
* **Weakness**: When streaming text (without `--json-output`), a hard-coded closure string (`"-" * 40`) is appended to the end of the stream. If a user pipes `walkie ask --stream` into another command, the hyphens corrupt the output. 
* **Suggestion**: Omit UI decorations completely when `sys.stdout.isatty()` is `False`. 

### 8. Logging & diagnostics
* **Weakness**: Currently, full prompt contents and full responses are logged to JSON and markdown files. For long context windows (e.g., 1M tokens), a single query can generate hundreds of megabytes of logs, filling the disk. 
* **Suggestion**: Add a `--no-log` flag to disable logging for high-volume/automated queries, and an environment variable override for the log directory.

### 9. Provider extensibility
* **Weakness**: `route_model` has a hardcoded `if/elif` block for ZenMux, NVIDIA, and other custom prefixes. Adding a new provider requires modifying the core routing logic. 
* **Suggestion**: Tie routing to the `PROVIDERS` dictionary. If a model starts with a provider prefix, dynamically pick the `api_base` and `api_key` from the config rather than hardcoding it.

### 10. Code quality & maintainability
* **Weakness**: The `ask` command is a 150-line monolith handling stdin parsing, file reading, chunking, routing, API calls, and logging. 
* **Suggestion**: Break it down into helper functions (`build_prompt`, `handle_streaming`, `log_interaction`). 

---

### Unified Code Diff / Refactoring

Below is the updated code applying these improvements:

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    # 4. Token Efficiency: Note that naive regex may break complex strings, 
    # but is acceptable for lightweight token reduction.
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')
    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        code = re.sub(pattern, lambda m: '' if m.group(0).startswith(('/*', '//')) else m.group(0), code)
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        code = re.sub(pattern, lambda m: '' if m.group(0).startswith('#') else m.group(0), code)

    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("")
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

# 9. Extensibility: Dynamic model routing
def route_model(model):
    """Dynamically route model based on PROVIDERS dict prefixes."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None
    routed_model = model

    for prov, cfg in PROVIDERS.items():
        prefix = f"{prov.lower()}/"
        if model.startswith(prefix):
            routed_model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
            api_base = cfg.get("api_base")
            if prov == "NVIDIA" and "deepseek" in routed_model.lower():
                api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv(cfg["env_var"])
            else:
                api_key = os.getenv(cfg["env_var"])
            break

    return routed_model, api_base, api_key

# 10. Quality: Modular ask command
def build_prompt(prompt, prompt_file, attach, strip_comments):
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:

            full_prompt = f"{full_prompt}\n\n{file_content}" if full_prompt else file_content
    if stdin_content:
        full_prompt = f"{full_prompt}\n\n{stdin_content}" if full_prompt else stdin_content

    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)
                attachment_blocks.append(f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n{file_content}\n```")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read {file_path}: {e}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:

Streaming Reliability\n\n**Weaknesses:**\n- Stream chunk parsing has bare `except Exception: pass`\n- No handling of interrupted streams\n- Usage data collection fragile across chunk formats\n- No partial response recovery on stream failure\n- Streaming errors hidden from user\n\n**Improvements:**\n```python\n# Robust streaming handler\nclass StreamHandler:\n    def __init__(self, model: str, json_output: bool):\n        self.model = model\n        self.json_output = json_output\n        self.chunks = []\n        self.usage_data = {}\n        self.error_chunks = 0\n        self.max_error_chunks = 5\n        \n    def process_chunk(self, chunk) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Process a stream chunk safely.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if not hasattr(chunk, 'choices') or not chunk.choices:\n                return None\n            \n            delta = chunk.choices[0].delta\n            \n            # def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', default="nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2", help="Model name (defaults to nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Determine max characters allowed for attachments based on model context limit
    # 1 token ≈ 4 characters in English text / code
    max_chars = 300000  # Default: ~100k tokens (120k tokens context window)
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000  # 1M+ context
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000  # 200k context
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000   # 8k context (safety limit)
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000   # 16k context

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                # Context-aware chunking/truncating specifically to different models
                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    # Find the nearest newline boundary strictly under max_chars to keep lines complete
                    trunc_idx = file_content.rfind('\n', 0, max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        # Fallback to finding the first newline after max_chars if none exists before it
                        trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = max_chars

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                try:
                    if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                        delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                        content_chunk = getattr(delta, 'content', None)
                        if content_chunk:
                            chunks.append(content_chunk)
                            if not json_output:
                                click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            if not stream:
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## Response
I'll audit `walkie.py` across all 10 perspectives and provide concrete improvements.

## 1. Non-tech User Friendliness

**Weaknesses:**
- Error messages are technical (raw API errors, stack traces)
- No example commands or quick-start guide
- `--extra-body` requires JSON knowledge
- Model aliases aren't explained
- No progress indicator for non-streaming mode

**Improvements:**
```python
# Add a friendly 'examples' command
@cli.command()
def examples():
    """Show common usage examples."""
    click.secho("🔊 Walkie-Talkie Examples:", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("""
  Basic question:
    walkie ask -p "Explain quantum computing"

  With attachment:
    walkie ask -p "Review this code" -a src/main.py --strip-comments

  Pipe from terminal:
    cat error.log | walkie ask -p "What's wrong?" -s "You are a DevOps expert"

  Different models:
    walkie ask -m openai/gpt-4 -p "Summarize this"
    walkie ask -m gemini/gemini-1.5-pro -p "Analyze trends"
""")

# Add user-friendly error messages
USER_FRIENDLY_ERRORS = {
    "Rate limit": "The API is busy. Please wait a moment and try again.",
    "Invalid API Key": "Your API key seems incorrect. Run 'walkie setup' to reconfigure.",
    "ConnectionError": "Network issue detected. Check your internet connection.",
    "timeout": "The request timed out. Try with a simpler/shorter prompt.",
}

def _get_friendly_error(exception_str: str) -> str:
    """Map technical errors to user-friendly messages."""
    for pattern, message in USER_FRIENDLY_ERRORS.items():
        if pattern.lower() in exception_str.lower():
            return message
    return f"Something went wrong: {exception_str[:200]}"
```

## 2. Antigravity IDE Agent Compatibility

**Weaknesses:**
- No structured exit codes for IDE parsing

- Progress/stderr mixing makes IDE parsing difficult
- No `--raw` flag for clean machine-readable output
- No stdin/stdout contract documentation

## 3. Security & API Safety

**Weaknesses:**
- API keys logged in environment variables visible in process
- No secret redaction in logs
- File attachments read blindly without size limits per file
- No path traversal protection for attachments
- `.env` file permissions only set on Unix, not Windows

**Improvements:**
```python
# Add security module
import secrets
from typing import Optional

class SecurityConfig:
    MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB = 10
    ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {
        '.py', '.js', '.ts', '.txt', '.md', '.yaml', '.yml',
        '.json', '.toml', '.ini', '.cfg', '.sh', '.rb',
        '.go', '.rs', '.c', '.h', '.cpp', '.java', '.kt'
    }
    FORBIDDEN_PATHS = {'/etc', '/proc', '/sys', 'C:\\Windows'}

def sanitize_for_log(text: str, api_keys: dict) -> str:
    """Redact API keys from logged content."""
    for key_name, key_value in api_keys.items():
        if key_value and len(key_value) > 8:
            text = text.replace(key_value, f"[REDACTED_{key_name}]")
    return text

def validate_attachment_path(file_path: str) -> bool:
    """Security check for attachment paths."""
    path = Path(file_path).resolve()
    
    # Check for path traversal
    if '..' in str(path):
        click.secho(f"Security: Path traversal detected in {file_path}", fg="red")
        return False
    
    # Check forbidden paths
    for forbidden in SecurityConfig.FORBIDDEN_PATHS:
        if str(path).startswith(forbidden):
            click.secho(f"Security: Forbidden path {file_path}", fg="red")
            return False
    
    return True

# In ask() file reading:
if not validate_attachment_path(str(path_obj)):
    continue

if path_obj.stat().st_size > SecurityConfig.MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB * 1024 * 1024:
    click.secho(f"Warning: Skipping {file_path} - exceeds {SecurityConfig.MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB}MB limit", fg="yellow")
    continue

# Log sanitization before writing:
log_data["user_prompt"] = sanitize_for_log(full_prompt, {
    k: os.getenv(v["env_var"]) for k, v in PROVIDERS.items()
})
```

## 4. Token & Context Window Efficiency

**Weaknesses:**
- Character-based truncation inaccurate (token ≠ character)
- No token counting before sending
- Comment stripping regex fragile and slow for large files
- No prompt compression strategies
- Context window limits hardcoded instead of queried

**Improvements:**
```python
# Add proper token estimation
import tiktoken

def estimate_tokens(text: str, model: str = "gpt-3.5-turbo") -> int:
    """Estimate token count for a given model."""
    try:
        # Try model-specific encoding
        encoding = tiktoken.encoding_for_model(model.replace("openai/", ""))
    except KeyError:
        # Fallback to cl100k_base for most modern models
        encoding = tiktoken.get_encoding("cl100k_base")
    return len(encoding.encode(text))

def chunk_attachment(content: str, max_tokens: int, model: str) -> str:
    """Intelligently chunk attachment to fit token budget."""
    tokens = estimate_tokens(content, model)
    if tokens <= max_tokens:
        return content
    
    # Binary search for token boundary
    chars_per_token_estimate = len(content) / tokens
    target_chars = int(max_tokens * chars_per_token_estimate * 0.9)  # 90% margin
    
    # Find newline boundary
    trunc_idx = content.rfind('\n', 0, target_chars)
    if trunc_idx == -1:
        trunc_idx = content.find('\n', target_chars)
    if trunc_idx == -1:
        trunc_idx = target_chars
    
    truncated = content[:trunc_idx]
    actual_tokens = estimate_tokens(truncated, model)
    
    return truncated + f"\n\n[Truncated: {tokens - actual_tokens} tokens removed]"

# In ask(), replace character-based truncation:
max_tokens_for_attachments = 5000  # Budget for attachments
if strip_comments:
    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)
file_content = chunk_attachment(file_content, max_tokens_for_attachments, model)
```

## 5. Streaming Reliability

**Weaknesses:**
- Stream chunk parsing has bare `except Exception: pass`
- No handling of interrupted streams
- Usage data collection fragile across chunk formats
- No partial response recovery on stream failure
- Streaming errors hidden from user

**Improvements:**
```python
# Robust streaming handler
class StreamHandler:
    def __init__(self, model: str, json_output: bool):
        self.model = model
        self.json_output = json_output
        self.chunks = []
        self.usage_data = {}
        self.error_chunks = 0
        self.max_error_chunks = 5
        
    def process_chunk(self, chunk) -> Optional[str]:
        """Process a stream chunk safely."""
        try:
            if not hasattr(chunk, 'choices') or not chunk.choices:
                return None
            
            delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
            
            # Handle content
            content = None
            if hasattr(delta, 'content'):
                content = delta.content
            elif isinstance(delta, dict) and 'content' in delta:
                content = delta['content']
                
            # Handle usage (final chunk often has usage)
            if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                self._extract_usage(chunk.usage)
                
            return content
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.error_chunks += 1
            if self.error_chunks > self.max_error_chunks:
                raise RuntimeError(f"Too many chunk errors: {e}")
            return None
    
    def _extract_usage(self, usage):
        """Extract usage data from various formats."""
        extractors = [
            lambda u: u.model_dump() if hasattr(u, 'model_dump') else None,
            lambda u: u.dict() if hasattr(u, 'dict') else None,
            lambda u: dict(u) if isinstance(u, dict) else None,
            lambda u: {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(u).items()} if hasattr(u, '__dict__') else None
        ]
        for extractor in extractors:
            try:
                data = extractor(usage)
                if data:
                    self.usage_data = data
                    return
            except:
                continue
    
    def get_response(self) -> tuple[str, dict]:
        """Get final response and usage."""
        return "".join(filter(None, self.chunks)), self.usage_data

# In ask() streaming:
handler = StreamHandler(model, json_output)
try:
    response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
    for chunk in response_stream:
        content = handler.process_chunk(chunk)
        if content and not json_output:
            click.echo(content, nl=False)
        if content:
            handler.chunks.append(content)
except KeyboardInterrupt:
    click.secho("\n\nStream interrupted by user", fg="yellow")
    # Still return what we got
except Exception as e:
    click.secho(f"Stream error: {e}", fg="red")
    # Return partial response
finally:
    reply, usage_data = handler.get_response()
```

## 6. Robust Error Handling

**Weaknesses:**
- No retry logic for transient failures
- No graceful degradation for missing optional dependencies
- `litellm` import failure unhandled
- File encoding errors silently ignored (`errors='ignore'`)
- No timeout configuration

**Improvements:**

  "response": "Here is the audit of the script. We identified a critical syntax bug, safety issues in the regex parser, and some robustness issues. \n\n### Identified Issues & Fixes:\n\n1. **SyntaxError on `full_prompt` string literal**:\n   In the original script, the string formatting for the attachment propagation is incomplete:\n   ```python\n   attachment_blocks.append(\n       f\"\\n---\\nFile: {path_obj.name}\\n```\"\n       f\"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\\n\"\n       f\"{file_content}\\n```\"\n   )\n   if attachment_blocks:\n       full_prompt += \"\\n\\n\n   ```\n   This will break Python execution. It needs to be completed as `full_prompt += \"\\n\\n\" + \"\\n\".join(attachment_blocks)`.\n\n2. **Regex stripping comments inside quoted string literals**:\n   For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML, the pattern used `(\\\"\\\"\\\"[\\s\\S]*?\\\"\\\"\\\"|\\'\\'\\'[\\s\\S]*?\\'\\'\\'|\\\"[^\\\"]*?\\\"|\\'[^\\']*?\\'|#.*)`. Since `#.*` is evaluated on its own (and doesn't require a preceding character like `(?<!:)//`), a `#` character occurring inside a single or double-quoted string literal can cause it to match independently and wrongly strip part of the string. Wrapping the `#` match inside `(?!['\"])` ensures that any `#` starting inside an existing literal isn't stripped:\n   `(?<!['\\\"])#.*` \n\n3. **Missing fallback for `max_tokens`**:\n   For models/execution paths missing max-token sizes, you can end up returning 0 tokens or defaulting to whatever system strict minimum exists. Setting `max_tokens` to `3000` inside the `ask` loop if `None` provides robust sizing.\n\n4. **`lazy_load_dotenv ImportError` Issue**:\n   If `python-dotenv` is not installed or not initialized, `set_key` fails namespace checks and raises an `ImportError`.     "completion_tokens": 2500,
    "prompt_tokens": 4512,
    "total_tokens": 7012,
    "completion_tokens_details": null,
    "prompt_tokens_details": null
  }
}
