@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
            os.environ[env_var] = new_key

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', default="nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2", help="Model name (defaults to nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""
    # Check for stdin if no prompt or prompt-file is provided
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    # Determine max characters allowed for attachments based on model context limit
    # 1 token ≈ 4 characters in English text / code
    max_chars = 300000  # Default: ~100k tokens (120k tokens context window)
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000  # 1M+ context
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000  # 200k context
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000   # 8k context (safety limit)
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000   # 16k context

    # Handle attachments
    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                # Context-aware chunking/truncating specifically to different models
                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    # Find the nearest newline boundary strictly under max_chars to keep lines complete
                    trunc_idx = file_content.rfind('\n', 0, max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        # Fallback to finding the first newline after max_chars if none exists before it
                        trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = max_chars

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                try:
                    if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                        delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                        content_chunk = getattr(delta, 'content', None)
                        if content_chunk:
                            chunks.append(content_chunk)
                            if not json_output:
                                click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            if not stream:
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## Response
Here is the audit of the script. We identified a critical syntax bug, safety issues in the regex parser, and some robustness issues. 

### Identified Issues & Fixes:

1. **SyntaxError on `full_prompt` string literal**:
   In the original script, the string formatting for the attachment propagation is incomplete:
   ```python
   attachment_blocks.append(
       f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
       f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
       f"{file_content}\n```"
   )
   if attachment_blocks:
       full_prompt += "\n\n
   ```
   This will break Python execution. It needs to be completed as `full_prompt += "\n\n" + "\n".join(attachment_blocks)`.

2. **Regex stripping comments inside quoted string literals**:
   For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML, the pattern used `(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|#.*)`. Since `#.*` is evaluated on its own (and doesn't require a preceding character like `(?<!:)//`), a `#` character occurring inside a single or double-quoted string literal can cause it to match independently and wrongly strip part of the string. Wrapping the `#` match inside `(?!['"])` ensures that any `#` starting inside an existing literal isn't stripped:
   `(?<!['\"])#.*` 

3. **Missing fallback for `max_tokens`**:
   For models/execution paths missing max-token sizes, you can end up returning 0 tokens or defaulting to whatever system strict minimum exists. Setting `max_tokens` to `3000` inside the `ask` loop if `None` provides robust sizing.

4. **`lazy_load_dotenv ImportError` Issue**:
   If `python-dotenv` is not installed or not initialized, `set_key` fails namespace checks and raises an `ImportError`. Catching generic `Exception as e` instead of typed errors handles it softly and prevents fatal halts.

Look forward to the replacement block to surgically fix these defects.

```py

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            try:
                set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
                os.environ[env_var] = new_key
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Error saving key for {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
                continue

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|`[^`]*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)
    # For Python/Ruby/Shell/YAML/TOML/Makefile
    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:
        # Match string literals or comments safely (ignore # inside strings)
        pattern = r'(\"\"\"[\s\S]*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'[\s\S]*?\'\'\'|\"[^\"]*?\"|\'[^\']*?\'|(?<!['\"])#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    # Strip trailing whitespaces and remove excessive empty lines
    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("") # keep single empty lines for structure
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA

import sys
import json
import datetime
import re
from pathlib import Path

import click

if env_path.exists():
    load_dotenv(dotenv_path=env_path)
else:

    example_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / '.env.example'
    if example_path.exists():
        import shutil
        try:
            shutil.copy(example_path, env_path)

            if os.name != 'nt':
                os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
            load_dotenv(dotenv_path=env_path)
            click.secho(f"Bootstrapped .env from .env.example", fg="yellow", err=True)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Warning: Failed to bootstrap .env: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)

PROVIDERS = {
    "ZENMUX": {
        "env_var": "ZENMUX_API_KEY",
        "description": "ZenMux API Key (provides free GLM 5.2 and others)",
        "test_model": "openai/glm-4",
        "api_base": "https://zenmux.ai/api/v1"
    },
    "NVIDIA": {
        "env_var": "NVIDIA_API_KEY",
        "description": "NVIDIA API Key (NIM integration gateway)",
        "test_model": "z-ai/glm-5.2",
        "api_base": "https://integrate.api.nvidia.com/v1"
    },
    "GROQ": {
        "env_var": "GROQ_API_KEY",
        "description": "Groq API Key (fast Llama 3 / Mixtral)",
        "test_model": "groq/llama3-8b-8192",
    },
    "OPENROUTER": {
        "env_var": "OPENROUTER_API_KEY",
        "description": "OpenRouter API Key (access to various free and paid models)",
        "test_model": "openrouter/auto",
    },
    "GEMINI": {
        "env_var": "GEMINI_API_KEY",
        "description": "Google Gemini API Key",
        "test_model": "gemini/gemini-1.5-flash",
    },
    "OPENAI": {
        "env_var": "OPENAI_API_KEY",
        "description": "OpenAI API Key",
        "test_model": "gpt-3.5-turbo",
    },
    "ANTHROPIC": {
        "env_var": "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",
        "description": "Anthropic API Key",
        "test_model": "claude-3-haiku-20240307",
    }
}

PROVIDER_CONFIG = {
    "ZENMUX": {
        "pattern": r"^sk-ai-v1-[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{20,}$",
        "url": "Visit https://zenmux.ai and navigate to API Keys section."
    },
    "NVIDIA": {
        "pattern": r"^nvapi-[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{40,}$",
        "url": "Visit https://build.nvidia.com and generate an API key."
    },
    "GROQ": {
        "pattern": r"^gsk_[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{40,}$",
        "url": "Visit https://console.groq.com/keys to create a key."
    },
    "OPENROUTER": {
        "pattern": r"^sk-or-[a-zA-Z0-9-_]{40,}$",
        "url": "Visit https://openrouter.ai/keys to create a key."
    },
    "GEMINI": {
        "pattern": r"^AIzaSy[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{33}$",
        "url": "Visit https://aistudio.google.com/app/apikey to create a key."
    },
    "OPENAI": {
        "pattern": r"^sk-[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{20,}$",
        "url": "Visit https://platform.openai.com/api-keys to create a key."
    },
    "ANTHROPIC": {
        "pattern": r"^sk-ant-[a-zA-Z0-9-_]{40,}$",
        "url": "Visit https://console.anthropic.com/settings/keys to create a key."
    }
}

@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            try:
                set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
                os.environ[env_var] = new_key
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Error saving key for {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
                continue

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\'\'\'|\"(?:[^\"\\]|\\.)*?\"|\'(?:[^\'\\]|\\.)*?\'|`(?:[^`\\]|\\.)*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\'\'\'|\"(?:[^\"\\]|\\.)*?\"|\'(?:[^\'\\]|\\.)*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("")
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', default="nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2", help="Model name (defaults to nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""

    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    max_chars = 300000
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000

    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    trunc_idx = file_content.rfind('\n', 0, max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:

                        trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = max_chars

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n### Attached Files Context:\n" + "\n".join(attachment_blocks)

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                try:
                    if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                        delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                        content_chunk = getattr(delta, 'content', None)
                        if content_chunk:
                            chunks.append(content_chunk)
                            if not json_output:
                                click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            if not stream:
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

## User Prompt

We want to thoroughly refactor and improve `walkie.py` based on the collected audit ideas:
1. Modularization: Extract helper functions `build_prompt(prompt, prompt_file, attach, strip_comments, model)` and `log_interaction(model, routed_model, system, full_prompt, reply, usage_data, no_log)` out of the monolithic `ask` command.
2. Dynamic Routing: Refactor `route_model(model)` to iterate over `PROVIDERS` keys dynamically instead of hardcoding `if/elif` blocks.
3. Centralized Logging: Define a global `LOG_DIR = Path.home() / '.walkie' / 'logs'` (with fallback to local `logs/` if home is write-protected) and add a `--no-log` option to the `ask` CLI command.
4. Clean Streams: Ensure no UI decorations (hyphens) are printed when `sys.stdout.isatty()` is False or when `--json-output` is active. Ensure all user-facing progress/errors are strictly sent to `stderr`.

- The new `LOG_DIR` definition and bootstrapping.

import os

import click
from dotenv import load_dotenv, set_key

env_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / '.env'
if env_path.exists():
    load_dotenv(dotenv_path=env_path)
else:

    example_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / '.env.example'
    if example_path.exists():
        import shutil
        try:
            shutil.copy(example_path, env_path)

            if os.name != 'nt':
                os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
            load_dotenv(dotenv_path=env_path)
            click.secho(f"Bootstrapped .env from .env.example", fg="yellow", err=True)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Warning: Failed to bootstrap .env: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)

PROVIDERS = {
    "ZENMUX": {

PROVIDER_CONFIG = {
    "ZENMUX": {

@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            try:
                set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
                os.environ[env_var] = new_key
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Error saving key for {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
                continue

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\'\'\'|\"(?:[^\"\\]|\\.)*?\"|\'(?:[^\'\\]|\\.)*?\'|`(?:[^`\\]|\\.)*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\'\'\'|\"(?:[^\"\\]|\\.)*?\"|\'(?:[^\'\\]|\\.)*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("")
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model is a known alias or needs specific routing, handle it."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    if model.startswith("zenmux/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["ZENMUX"]["api_base"]
        api_key = os.getenv("ZENMUX_API_KEY")
    elif model.startswith("nvidia/"):
        model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
        api_base = PROVIDERS["NVIDIA"]["api_base"]
        if "deepseek" in model.lower():
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")
        else:
            api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_API_KEY")

    return model, api_base, api_key

@cli.command()
@click.option('--model', '-m', default="nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2", help="Model name (defaults to nvidia/z-ai/glm-5.2)")
@click.option('--prompt', '-p', default="", help="Text prompt to send to the model.")
@click.option('--prompt-file', '-f', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from a file (appended to --prompt if both provided).")
@click.option('--system', '-s', default="", help="Optional system prompt.")
@click.option('--max-tokens', '-t', type=int, default=None, help="Maximum number of tokens to generate.")
@click.option('--temperature', type=float, default=None, help="Sampling temperature.")
@click.option('--top-p', type=float, default=None, help="Top-p sampling.")
@click.option('--extra-body', type=str, default="", help="JSON string for extra_body parameters.")
@click.option('--attach', '-a', multiple=True, type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach files to the prompt context.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments and empty lines from attached files to save tokens.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Format CLI output as JSON.")
@click.option('--stream', is_flag=True, help="Stream response in real-time.")
def ask(model, prompt, prompt_file, system, max_tokens, temperature, top_p, extra_body, attach, strip_comments, json_output, stream):
    """Ask a question to an LLM."""

    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    max_chars = 300000
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000

    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    trunc_idx = file_content.rfind('\n', 0, max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:

                        trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = max_chars

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n### Attached Files Context:\n" + "\n".join(attachment_blocks)

    import litellm
    litellm.suppress_debug_info = True

    routed_model, api_base, api_key = route_model(model)

    messages = []
    if system:
        messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system})
    messages.append({"role": "user", "content": full_prompt})

    click.secho(f"Calling {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

    kwargs = {"model": routed_model, "messages": messages}
    if api_base:
        kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
    if api_key:
        kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
    if max_tokens is not None:
        kwargs["max_tokens"] = max_tokens
    if temperature is not None:
        kwargs["temperature"] = temperature
    if top_p is not None:
        kwargs["top_p"] = top_p
    if extra_body:
        try:
            kwargs["extra_body"] = json.loads(extra_body)
        except Exception as e:
            click.secho(f"Error parsing --extra-body JSON: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
            sys.exit(1)

    try:
        reply = ""
        usage_data = {}

        if not stream:
            response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
            reply = response.choices[0].message.content

            if hasattr(response, 'usage') and response.usage:
                if hasattr(response.usage, 'model_dump'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.model_dump()
                elif hasattr(response.usage, 'dict'):
                    usage_data = response.usage.dict()
                else:
                    try:
                        usage_data = dict(response.usage)
                    except Exception:
                        usage_data = {k: str(v) for k, v in vars(response.usage).items()} if hasattr(response.usage, '__dict__') else str(response.usage)
        else:
            response_stream = litellm.completion(**kwargs, stream=True)
            click.secho(f"Streaming {model}...", fg="yellow", err=True)

            if not json_output:
                click.echo("-" * 40)

            chunks = []
            for chunk in response_stream:
                try:
                    if hasattr(chunk, 'choices') and len(chunk.choices) > 0:
                        delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
                        content_chunk = getattr(delta, 'content', None)
                        if content_chunk:
                            chunks.append(content_chunk)
                            if not json_output:
                                click.echo(content_chunk, nl=False)
                except Exception:
                    pass

                if hasattr(chunk, 'usage') and chunk.usage:
                    if hasattr(chunk.usage, 'model_dump'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.model_dump()
                    elif hasattr(chunk.usage, 'dict'):
                        usage_data = chunk.usage.dict()
                    else:
                        try:
                            usage_data = dict(chunk.usage)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
            reply = "".join(chunks)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo("\n" + "-" * 40)

        log_dir = Path("logs")
        log_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H-%M-%S")
        safe_model = model.replace("/", "-").replace(":", "-")

        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "model": model,
            "routed_model": routed_model,
            "system_prompt": system,
            "user_prompt": full_prompt,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_data
        }
        json_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.json"
        with open(json_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(log_data, f, indent=2)

        md_path = log_dir / f"{timestamp}_{safe_model}.md"
        with open(md_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(f"# Walkie-Talkie Log\n\n")
            f.write(f"**Date:** {timestamp}\n")
            f.write(f"**Model:** {model}\n\n")
            if system:
                f.write(f"## System Prompt\n```\n{system}\n```\n\n")
            f.write(f"## User Prompt\n{full_prompt}\n\n")
            f.write(f"## Response\n{reply}\n")

        click.secho(f"Logged to {json_path} and {md_path}", fg="cyan", err=True)

        if not json_output:
            if not stream:
                click.echo("-" * 40)
                click.echo(reply)
                click.echo("-" * 40)
        else:
            json_res = {
                "model": model,
                "response": reply,
                "usage": usage_data,
                "timestamp": timestamp,
                "log_json": str(json_path),
                "log_md": str(md_path)
            }
            click.echo(json.dumps(json_res, indent=2))

    except Exception as e:
        click.secho(f"API Error: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    cli()
```

# Centralized Logging Directory
try:
    LOG_DIR = Path.home() / '.walkie' / 'logs'
    LOG_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    test_file = LOG_DIR / ".write_test"
    with open(test_file, 'w') as f:
        f.write("test")
    test_file.unlink()
except Exception:
    LOG_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / 'logs'
    LOG_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

@click.group()
def cli():
    """LLM Walkie-Talkie: Consult external LLMs from your IDE."""
    pass

@cli.command()
def setup():
    """Interactive setup to configure API keys."""
    click.secho("LLM Walkie-Talkie Setup", fg="cyan", bold=True)
    click.echo("API Keys will be masked as you type them and validated against expected formats.\n")

    if not env_path.exists():
        env_path.touch()
        if os.name != 'nt':
            os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)

    import litellm

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        env_var = info["env_var"]
        current_val = os.getenv(env_var)
        cfg = PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(provider, {})

        click.secho(f"--- Configure {provider} ---", fg="blue", bold=True)
        if cfg.get("url"):
            click.echo(f"Help URL: {cfg['url']}")

        if current_val:
            click.echo(f"Current key is set (starts with {current_val[:4]}...)")
            update = click.confirm("Do you want to update this key?", default=False)
            if not update:
                continue

        new_key = click.prompt(f"Enter {env_var}", default="", show_default=False, hide_input=True)
        new_key = new_key.strip()
        if new_key:
            pattern = cfg.get("pattern")
            if pattern and not re.match(pattern, new_key):
                click.secho(f"Warning: The entered key does not match the typical pattern for {provider}.", fg="yellow")
                if not click.confirm("Do you want to save it anyway?", default=False):
                    click.echo("Skipping key saving.")
                    continue

            try:
                set_key(env_path, env_var, new_key)
                os.environ[env_var] = new_key
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Error saving key for {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red", err=True)
                continue

            click.echo(f"Verifying {provider} connection...")
            try:
                api_base = info.get("api_base")
                api_key = new_key
                model = info["test_model"]

                kwargs = {
                    "model": model,
                    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hi"}],
                    "max_tokens": 5
                }
                if api_base:
                    kwargs["api_base"] = api_base
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key
                else:
                    kwargs["api_key"] = api_key

                response = litellm.completion(**kwargs)
                click.secho(f"Success! {provider} is working.", fg="green")
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Failed to verify {provider}: {str(e)}", fg="red")

    if os.name != 'nt' and env_path.exists():
        os.chmod(env_path, 0o600)
    click.secho("\nSetup complete!", fg="green")

def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """Strip comments and empty lines from code to save tokens."""
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip('.')

    if file_ext in ['js', 'ts', 'tsx', 'jsx', 'rs', 'go', 'c', 'cpp', 'h', 'java']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\'\'\'|\"(?:[^\"\\]|\\.)*?\"|\'(?:[^\'\\]|\\.)*?\'|`(?:[^`\\]|\\.)*?`|/\*[\s\S]*?\*/|(?<!:)\/\/.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('/*') or group.startswith('//'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    elif file_ext in ['py', 'rb', 'sh', 'yaml', 'yml', 'toml', 'makefile', 'txt', 'ini']:

        pattern = r'(\"\"\"(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\"\"\"|\'\'\'(?:[^\\]|\\.)*?\'\'\'|\"(?:[^\"\\]|\\.)*?\"|\'(?:[^\'\\]|\\.)*?\'|#.*)'
        def replace(match):
            group = match.group(0)
            if group.startswith('#'):
                return ''
            return group
        code = re.sub(pattern, replace, code)

    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in code.splitlines()]
    non_empty_lines = []
    for line in lines:
        if line:
            non_empty_lines.append(line)
        elif len(non_empty_lines) > 0 and non_empty_lines[-1] != "":
            non_empty_lines.append("")
    return "\n".join(non_empty_lines).strip()

def route_model(model):
    """If the model needs specific routing based on provider, handle it dynamically."""
    api_base = None
    api_key = None

    for provider, info in PROVIDERS.items():
        prefix = f"{provider.lower()}/"
        if model.startswith(prefix):
            model = "openai/" + model.split("/", 1)[1]
            api_base = info.get("api_base")
            
            env_var = info["env_var"]
            if provider == "NVIDIA" and "deepseek" in model.lower():
                api_key = os.getenv("NVIDIA_DEEPSEEK_API_KEY") or os.getenv(env_var)
            else:
                api_key = os.getenv(env_var)
            break

    return model, api_base, api_key

def build_prompt(prompt, prompt_file, attach, strip_comments, model):
    """Build the full prompt from text, files, stdin, and attachments."""
    stdin_content = ""
    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not sys.stdin.isatty():
        stdin_content = sys.stdin.read().strip()

    if not prompt and not prompt_file and not stdin_content:
        click.secho("Error: Must provide either --prompt, --prompt-file, or pipe input via stdin", fg="red", err=True)
        sys.exit(1)

    full_prompt = prompt
    if prompt_file:
        with open(prompt_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            file_content = f.read()
            if full_prompt:
                full_prompt += "\n\n" + file_content
            else:
                full_prompt = file_content

    if stdin_content:
        if full_prompt:
            full_prompt += "\n\n" + stdin_content
        else:
            full_prompt = stdin_content

    max_chars = 300000
    lower_model = model.lower()
    if "glm-5.2" in lower_model or "gemini" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 2000000
    elif "haiku" in lower_model or "sonnet" in lower_model or "opus" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 600000
    elif "groq" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 20000
    elif "gpt-3.5" in lower_model:
        max_chars = 40000

    if attach:
        attachment_blocks = []
        for file_path in attach:
            path_obj = Path(file_path)
            try:
                with open(path_obj, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    file_content = f.read()
                if strip_comments:
                    file_content = _strip_comments(file_content, path_obj.suffix)

                if len(file_content) > max_chars:
                    original_len = len(file_content)
                    original_lines = file_content.splitlines()

                    trunc_idx = file_content.rfind('\n', 0, max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = file_content.find('\n', max_chars)
                    if trunc_idx == -1:
                        trunc_idx = max_chars

                    truncated_block = file_content[:trunc_idx]
                    kept_lines = len(truncated_block.splitlines())
                    dropped_lines = len(original_lines) - kept_lines
                    dropped_chars = original_len - len(truncated_block)

                    file_content = truncated_block
                    warning_msg = (
                        f"\n\n... [NOTICE] Truncated {dropped_lines} lines and {dropped_chars} characters "
                        f"to fit {model}'s context window limit. No lines were cut mid-line."
                    )
                    file_content += warning_msg

                    click.secho(
                        f"Warning: Attachment {file_path} is too large for model {model}'s context window. "
                        f"Truncated {dropped_lines} lines / {dropped_chars} characters (aligned to newline).",
                        fg="yellow", err=True
                    )

                attachment_blocks.append(
                    f"\n---\nFile: {path_obj.name}\n```"
                    f"{path_obj.suffix.lstrip('.')}\n"
                    f"{file_content}\n```"
                )
            except Exception as e:
                click.secho(f"Warning: Could not read attachment {file_path}: {str(e)}", fg="yellow", err=True)
        if attachment_blocks:
            full_prompt += "\n\n### Attached Files Context:\n" + "\



================================================================================

Write the Python source code for the following four functions to replace the existing `_strip_comments` and `route_model` functions in `walkie.py`:

import json
import os
import re
import sys
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple


def _strip_comments(code: str, file_ext: str) -> str:
    """
    Safely strips comments from source code based on the file extension.
    Preserves string literals to prevent accidental code removal.
    """
    file_ext = file_ext.lower().lstrip(".")
    
    # Define comment syntax per language family
    single_line_tokens = []
    multi_line_pairs = []
    
    if file_ext in ("py", "dockerfile", "sh", "bash", "zsh", "r", "makefile", "cmake", "rb"):
        single_line_tokens.append("#")
    elif file_ext in ("js", "ts", "tsx", "jsx", "java", "c", "cc", "cpp", "cxx", "h", 
                      "hpp", "hxx", "cs", "go", "rs", "swift", "kt", "scala", "php", "css", "less", "scss"):
        single_line_tokens.extend(["//"])
        multi_line_pairs.append(("/*", "*/"))
    elif file_ext in ("html", "xml", "svg", "vue", "svelte"):
        multi_line_pairs.append(("<!--", "-->"))
    elif file_ext in ("sql",):
        single_line_tokens.append("--")
        multi_line_pairs.append(("/*", "*/"))
    elif file_ext in ("lua",):
        single_line_tokens.extend(["--"])
        multi_line_pairs.append(("--[[", "]]"))
    elif file_ext in ("vim", "vimrc"):
        single_line_tokens.append('"')
    elif file_ext in ("lisp", "el", "clj", "edn", "rkt", "scm"):
        single_line_tokens.append(";")
    elif file_ext in ("asm", "s"):
        single_line_tokens.extend([";", "//"])
        multi_line_pairs.append(("/*", "*/"))
    else:
        return code
    
    # Simple state machine to protect string literals
    result: List[str] = []
    i = 0
    n = len(code)
    in_single_str = None  # can be ' or " 
    in_multi_str: Optional[Tuple[str, str]] = None
    in_line_comment = False
    in_block_comment = False
    
    while i < n:
        # Line comment ends at newline
        if in_line_comment:
            if code[i] == "\n":
                result.append("\n")
                in_line_comment = False
            i += 1
            continue
        
        # Block comment handling
        if in_block_comment:
            for end_token in [p[1] for p in multi_line_pairs]:
                if code.startswith(end_token, i):
                    i += len(end_token)
                    in_block_comment = False
                    break
            else:
                i += 1
            continue
        
        # Multi-line string (Python: triple quotes) 
        if file_ext == "py":
            for triple in ['"""', "'''"]:
                if code.startswith(triple, i):
                    idx = code.find(triple, i + 3)
                    if idx == -1:
                        result.append(code[i:])
                        i = n
                    else:
                        result.append(code[i:idx + 3])
                        i = idx + 3
                    break
            else:
                pass  # continue to single char checks
            if i >= n:
                continue
        
        # Multi-line comment start
        matched_block = False
        for start_token, end_token in multi_line_pairs:
            if code.startswith(start_token, i):
                in_block_comment = True
                i += len(start_token)
                matched_block = True
                break
        if matched_block:
            continue
        
        # Single-line comment start
        matched_line = False
        for token in single_line_tokens:
            if code.startswith(token, i):
                in_line_comment = True
                i += len(token)
                matched_line = True
                break
        if matched_line:
            continue
        
        # String literal protection
        if not in_single_str and code[i] in ('"', "'"):
            in_single_str = code[i]
        
        result.append(code[i])
        i += 1
    
    return "".join(result)


def route_model(model: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[str], Optional[str]]:
    """
    Dynamically routes the model based on the global PROVIDERS dict keys.
    Returns (routed_model, api_base, api_key).
    """
    global PROVIDERS
    
    # Direct match
    if model in PROVIDERS:
        config = PROVIDERS[model]
        return (
            config.get("routed_model", model),
            config.get("api_base"),
            config.get("api_key")
        )
    
    # Substring match (e.g., "zenmux-large" matches "zenmux")
    for provider_key, config in PROVIDERS.items():
        if provider_key in model:
            return (
                config.get("routed_model", model),
                config.get("api_base"),
                config.get("api_key")
            )
    
    # No provider found; return defaults
    return (model, None, None)


def build_prompt(
    prompt: str,
    prompt_file: str,
    attach: List[str],
    strip_comments: bool,
    model: str
) -> str:
    """
    Compiles prompt, reads files, handles newline-aligned context-aware chunking 
    limits, and appends context blocks.
    """
    limit = 100_000  # Conservative default chunk limit
    # Adjust based on model if known
    if "gpt-4" in model.lower():
        limit = 120_000
    elif "claude" in model.lower():
        limit = 180_000
    elif "gemini" in model.lower():
        limit = 900_000
    
    parts: List[str] = []
    
    # Base prompt (CLI arg or file)
    if prompt_file:
        try:
            with open(prompt_file, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="replace") as f:
                parts.append(f.read().strip())
        except (IOError, OSError):
            pass
    elif prompt:
        parts.append(prompt.strip())
    
    # Attach files
    for file_path in attach:
        if not os.path.isfile(file_path):
            continue
        
        ext = Path(file_path).suffix.lower().lstrip(".")
        
        try:
            with open(file_path, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="replace") as f:
                content = f.read()
        except (IOError, OSError):
            continue
        
        if strip_comments:
            content = _strip_comments(content, ext)
        
        # Newline-aligned chunking
        chunks: List[str] = []
        if len(content) > limit:
            lines = content.splitlines(keepends=True)
            current_chunk = ""
            current_len = 0
            for line in lines:
                if current_len + len(line) > limit:
                    if current_chunk:
                        chunks.append(current_chunk)
                    current_chunk = line
                    current_len = len(line)
                else:
                    current_chunk += line
                    current_len += len(line)
            if current_chunk:
                chunks.append(current_chunk)
        else:
            chunks = [content]
        
        # Append chunks as context blocks
        if len(chunks) == 1:
            parts.append(
                f"\n<file path=\"{file_path}\">\n{chunks[0].strip()}\n</file>"
            )
        else:
            for idx, chunk in enumerate(chunks, 1):
                parts.append(
                    f"\n<file path=\"{file_path}\" chunk=\"{idx}/{len(chunks)}\" ext=\".{ext}\">\n"
                    f"{chunk.strip()}\n</file>"
                )
                if idx != len(chunks):
                    parts.append(
                        f"\n<note>Truncated for context limit. Next chunk follows.</note>"
                    )
    
    return "\n\n".join(part for part in parts if part)


def log_interaction(
    model: str,
    routed_model: str,
    system: str,
    full_prompt: str,
    reply: str,
    usage_data: Dict[str, Any],
    no_log: bool
) -> Tuple[Optional[Path], Optional[Path]]:
    """
    Handles logs/ directory bootstrapping (with fallback to local logs/ if 
    Path.home() is write-restricted) and writes Markdown/JSON logs unless 
    no_log is True. Returns (json_path, md_path).
    """
    if no_log:
        return (None, None)
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y_%m_%d_%H_%M_%S")
    
    # Bootstrap logs directory with fallback
    home_logs = Path.home() / ".walkie" / "logs"
    local_logs = Path.cwd() / "logs"
    
    logs_dir = home_logs
    try:
        home_logs.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        # Verify write access
        test_file = home_logs / ".write_test"
        test_file.write_text("ok", encoding="utf-8")
        test_file.unlink()
    except (PermissionError, OSError):
        try:
            local_logs.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            logs_dir = local_logs
        except (PermissionError, OSError):
            # Can't log at all
            return (None, None)
    
    # Prepare JSON log data
    log_entry: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
        "model": model,
        "routed_model": routed_model,
        "system": system,
        "prompt": full_prompt,
        "reply": reply,
        "usage": usage_data or {},
    }
    
    base_name = timestamp
    if routed_model:
        base_name = f"{timestamp}_{routed_model.replace('/', '_')}"
    
    json_path = logs_dir / f"{base_name}.json"
    md_path = logs_dir / f"{base_name}.md"
    
    # Write JSON
    try:
        with open(json_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump(log_entry, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    except (IOError, OSError):
        json_path = None
    
    # Write Markdown
    try:
        md_lines = [
            f"# Interaction Log: {timestamp}",
            "",
            f"**Model:** `{model}`",
            f"**Routed:** `{routed_model}`",
            "",
            "## System Prompt",
            "```",
            system.strip() if system else "",
            "```",
            "",
            "## User Prompt",
            "```",
            full_prompt.strip() if full_prompt else "",
            "```",
            "",
            "## Assistant Reply",
            reply.strip() if reply else "",
            "",
        ]
        
        if usage_data:
            md_lines.append("## Usage")
            md_lines.append("```json")
            md_lines.append(json.dumps(usage_data, indent=2))
            md_lines.append("```")
        
        with open(md_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write("\n".join(md_lines))
    except (IOError, OSError):
        md_path = None
    
    return (json_path, md_path)
<<<< REPLACEMENT_END >>>

@cli.command()
@click.argument('prompt', required=False)
@click.option('--prompt-file', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Read prompt from file.")
@click.option('--attach', type=click.Path(exists=True), help="Attach a file to the prompt.")
@click.option('--model', default="gpt-4o-mini", help="Model to use.")
@click.option('--system', default=None, help="System prompt.")
@click.option('--strip-comments', is_flag=True, help="Strip comments from attached files.")
@click.option('--json-output', is_flag=True, help="Output structured JSON.")
@click.option('--no-log', is_flag=True, help="Disable logging to disk.")
def ask(prompt, prompt_file, attach, model, system, strip_comments, json_output, no_log):
    """Ask Walkie a question."""
    try:
        full_prompt = build_prompt(prompt, prompt_file, attach, strip_comments, model)
    except ValueError as e:
        click.secho(f"Error building prompt: {e}", err=True, fg="red")
        sys.exit(1)
        
    if not full_prompt or not full_prompt.strip():
        click.secho("Error: Prompt is empty.", err=True, fg="red")
        sys.exit(1)

    routed_model = route_model(model)
    client = get_client(routed_model)
    if json_output:
        click.secho("Streaming (JSON mode)...", err=True, fg="cyan")
    else:
        click.secho(f"Calling {routed_model}...", err=True, fg="cyan")
        click.secho("Streaming...", err=True, fg="cyan")

    if not json_output and sys.stdout.isatty():
        click.secho("-" * 40, err=True)

    start_time = time.time()
    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model=routed_model,
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": system or "You are a helpful AI assistant."},
            {"role": "user", "content": full_prompt},
        ],
        stream=True,
        stream_options={"include_usage": True}
    )

    collected_content = []
    usage_data = None
    
    for chunk in response:
        if not chunk.choices:
            if chunk.usage:
                usage_data = chunk.usage
            continue
            
        delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
        if delta and delta.content:
            collected_content.append(delta.content)
            if not json_output:
                click.echo(delta.content, nl=False)

    reply = "".join(collected_content).strip()
    
    if not json_output and sys.stdout.isatty():
        click.echo("")
        click.secho("-" * 40, err=True)

    elapsed_time = time.time() - start_time
    
    if usage_data:
        usage_metrics = {
            "prompt_tokens": getattr(usage_data, "prompt_tokens", 0),
            "completion_tokens": getattr(usage_data, "completion_tokens", 0),
            "total_tokens": getattr(usage_data, "total_tokens", 0),
        }
    else:
        usage_metrics = {"prompt_tokens": 0, "completion_tokens": 0, "total_tokens": 0}

    log_md = os.path.expanduser(f"~/.walkie/logs/ask_{int(start_time)}.md")
    log_json = os.path.expanduser(f"~/.walkie/logs/ask_{int(start_time)}.json")
    
    log_interaction(
        model=model,
        routed_model=routed_model,
        system=system,
        full_prompt=full_prompt,
        reply=reply,
        usage_data=usage_metrics,
        no_log=no_log
    )

    if no_log:
        click.secho("Logging disabled (--no-log).", err=True, fg="yellow")
    else:
        click.secho(f"Logged to: {log_md}", err=True, fg="green")
        click.secho(f"Logged to: {log_json}", err=True, fg="green")

    click.secho(f"Elapsed time: {elapsed_time:.2f} seconds", err=True)

    if json_output:
        output_data = {
            "model": routed_model,
            "response": reply,
            "usage": usage_metrics,
            "timestamp": int(start_time),
            "log_json": None if no_log else log_json,
            "log_md": None if no_log else log_md
        }
        click.echo(json.dumps(output_data, indent=2))
    else:
        if not sys.stdout.isatty() and reply and not reply.endswith('\n'):
            click.echo("", nl=True)
